<title>Document</title></head><body><div id="i258f796e8540472983406e92797901c7_1"></div><div style="min-height:54pt;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:3pt;text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:16pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">HealthEquity Reports Record HSA Sales, Asset Growth</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:3pt;text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Updates Previous Fiscal 2023 Guidance, Announces Investor Conferences, Presentations </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:6pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Draper, Utah &#8211; February 14, 2023 &#8211; HealthEquity, Inc. (NASDAQ&#58; HQY) (&#34;HealthEquity&#34; or the &#34;Company&#34;), the nation's largest health savings account (&#34;HSA&#34;) custodian, today announced HSA Assets and Total Accounts as of its fiscal year ended January&#160;31, 2023. The Company also updated its previously announced FY23 guidance and announced upcoming investor conferences and presentations.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:6pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The total number of HSAs as of January&#160;31, 2023, was 8.0 million, an increase of 11%, from 7.2 million as of January&#160;31, 2022. The Company closed its fiscal year 2023 with 14.9 million Total Accounts, an increase of 4%, from 14.4 million as of January&#160;31, 2022. HSA Assets grew to $22.1 billion as of January&#160;31, 2023, an increase of 13% from $19.6 billion a year earlier.</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8220;Team Purple finished fiscal 2023 with record sales of nearly 1 million new HSAs and with $22 billion of HSA assets,&#8221; said President and CEO Jon Kessler. &#8220;We are grateful to our many partners and clients working together with us to help an increasing number of American families connect health and wealth and enabling millions to achieve wellness today and financial well-being tomorrow.&#8221;</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:6pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Also commenting, Tyson Murdock, Executive Vice President and CFO of HealthEquity, said, &#8220;With the record-setting sales year we are reporting today, we expect to reach the top-end of previously provided ranges for revenue and earnings, including revenue of approximately $860 million for our fiscal year ended January 31, 2023. We provided initial guidance for fiscal 2024 on December 6, 2022, and expect to update that guidance in our Q4 earnings release scheduled for March 21, 2023.&#8221;</font></div><div
